country_event = {
	id = china_national_committee.02
	title = china_national_committee.02.t
	desc = china_national_committee.02.d
	picture = x
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_national_committee.02.a executed"
		name = china_national_committee.02.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}

}

country_event = {
	id = china_sar.001
	title = china_sar.001.t
	desc = china_sar.001.d
	picture = x
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = china_sar.001.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_sar.001.a executed"
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = CHI
			modifier = CSSTA
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = TAI
			modifier = CSSTA
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = CHI
			modifier = large_commercial_relations
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = TAI
			modifier = large_commercial_relations
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CHI_TAI_shared_modifier } } }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CHI_TAI_shared_modifier }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = { localization_key = modifies_dynamic_modifier_tt MODIFIER = CHI_TAI_shared_modifier }
		add_to_variable = { CHI_TAI_democratic_drift = -0.02 tooltip = democratic_drift_tt }
		add_to_variable = { CHI_TAI_civilian_factories_productivity = 0.03 tooltip = civilian_factories_productivity_tt }
		set_country_flag = TAI_CSSTA_signed
		CHI = { add_to_variable = { CHI_TAI_trust = 10 } }
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
	}

	option = {
		name = china_sar.001.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_sar.001.b executed"
		CHI = {
			add_to_variable = { CHI_TAI_trust = -5 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { CHI_TAI_trust < 0 } }
				set_variable = { CHI_TAI_trust = 0 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
	}

}

country_event = {
	id = china_sar.005
	title = china_sar.005.t
	desc = china_sar.005.d
	picture = x
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = china_sar.005.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_sar.005.a executed"
		set_country_flag = { flag = TAI_foreign_interference value = 1 days = 180 }
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = USA
			modifier = political_outreach
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = JAP
			modifier = political_outreach
		}
		CHI = {
			add_to_variable = { CHI_TAI_trust = -15 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { CHI_TAI_trust < 0 } }
				set_variable = { CHI_TAI_trust = 0 }
			}
			country_event = { id = china_sar.006 days = 3 }
		}
	}

}

	id = CHI_sco.10
	title = CHI_sco.10.t
	desc = CHI_sco.10.d
	picture = x
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = CHI_sco.10.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CHI_sco.10.a executed"
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		CHI_sco_promote_to_member = yes
		CHI = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = diplomatic_support
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = diplomatic_disloyalty
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				has_opinion = { target = CHI value > 50 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				has_opinion = { target = CHI value > 100 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = CHI_sco.10.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CHI_sco.10.b executed"
		CHI_sco_remove = yes
		SOV = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = has_expressed_loyalty
			}
		}
		CHI = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = resisted_territorial_ambition
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 40 }
	}

	option = {
		name = CHI_sco.10.c
		trigger = {
			has_opinion = { target = CHI value > 0 }
			has_opinion = { target = SOV value > 0 }
		}
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CHI_sco.10.c executed"
		CHI_sco_remove = yes
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
	}


}

		}

							on_lose = china_scs.58

							num_provinces = 1

							on_lose = china_scs.56
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {

					transfer_state = 943

				}

			AST = { add_war_support = 0.05 }
		}

			base = 20
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = VIE
					is_in_faction_with = PHI
					is_in_faction_with = MAY
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 15

					other = CHI
					ratio > 1.2
				}
			}

				add = 10
				OR = {

					PHI = { has_opinion = { target = USA value > 25 } }
					MAY = { has_opinion = { target = USA value > 25 } }
				}
			}

		clamp_variable = { var = CHI_chinese_aggression min = -50 max = 50 }

			limit = { has_country_flag = CHI_scs_ultimatum_issued_VIE }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { owns_state = 813 } }
				transfer_state = 813
			}
			add_state_core = 813
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CHI_scs_ultimatum_issued_PHI }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { owns_state = 943 } }

			}
			add_state_core = 943

		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CHI_scs_ultimatum_issued_MAY }

				limit = { NOT = { owns_state = 526 } }
				transfer_state = 526
			}
			add_state_core = 526
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			USA = { country_event = { id = china_scs.53 days = 7 } }
		}
	}

			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 813 }
				transfer_state = 813
				VIE = { add_state_core = 813 }
			}
			clr_country_flag = CHI_scs_ultimatum_issued_VIE

		if = {

				transfer_state = 943
				PHI = { add_state_core = 943 }
			}
			clr_country_flag = CHI_scs_ultimatum_issued_PHI

				transfer_state = 526
				MAY = { add_state_core = 526 }
			}
			clr_country_flag = CHI_scs_ultimatum_issued_MAY
		}
		clr_country_flag = CHI_scs_ultimatum_issued_any
		add_to_variable = { CHI_chinese_aggression = -8 tooltip = CHI_chinese_aggression_tt }
		clamp_variable = { var = CHI_chinese_aggression min = -50 max = 50 }
		add_to_variable = { CHI_scs_framework = 5 tooltip = CHI_scs_framework_tt }
		clamp_variable = { var = CHI_scs_framework min = -50 max = 50 }

			base = 20

					value = 35
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
		}
	}

		add_to_variable = { CHI_scs_framework = -15 tooltip = CHI_scs_framework_tt }

# Fires at the debtor the month it first misses a payment. The default flag gates the whole
# predatory branch, so both sides have to be told it happened.
country_event = {
	id = chi_bri.16
	title = chi_bri.16.t
	desc = chi_bri.16.d
	picture = x
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = chi_bri.16.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: chi_bri.16.a executed"
		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
	}

}

# Fires at the debtor when China claims resource rights. China has already decided to demand;
# this is the debtor's answer, because the concession idea is permanent.
country_event = {
	id = chi_bri.17
	title = chi_bri.17.t
	desc = chi_bri.17.d
	picture = x
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = chi_bri.17.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: chi_bri.17.a executed"
		CHI_bri_clear_loan = yes
		add_ideas = CHI_bri_resource_concession_idea
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = CHI modifier = medium_decrease }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				has_war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 3
				OR = {
					is_puppet_of = CHI
					is_in_faction_with = CHI
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_stability > 0.6
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = chi_bri.17.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: chi_bri.17.b executed"
		# Refusing keeps the debt and the default flag, which leaves Asset Seizure armed.
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_bri_refuse_concession_tt
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = CHI modifier = large_decrease }
		CHI = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = large_decrease }
			country_event = { id = chi_bri.18 days = 2 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 3
			modifier = {
				add = 4
				has_opinion = { target = CHI value < 0 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_puppet_of = CHI
			}
		}
	}

}

	id = CHI_semiconductor_events.1

	desc = CHI_semiconductor_events.1.d
	picture = x

	fire_only_once = yes

		name = CHI_semiconductor_events.1.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: CHI_semiconductor_events.1.o1"
		USA = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = CHI
				modifier = chi_usa_sanctions_response
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CHI_semiconductor_backwardness }
			custom_effect_tooltip = { localization_key = modifies_dynamic_modifier_tt MODIFIER = CHI_economy_modifier }
			add_to_variable = { CHI_economy_research_speed_factor = -0.08 tooltip = research_speed_factor_tt }
			add_to_variable = { CHI_economy_production_factory_max_efficiency_factor = -0.06 tooltip = production_factory_max_efficiency_factor_tt }
			add_to_variable = { CHI_economy_civilian_factories_productivity = -0.05 tooltip = civilian_factories_productivity_tt }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CHI_semiconductor_backwardness_2 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = { localization_key = modifies_dynamic_modifier_tt MODIFIER = CHI_economy_modifier }
			add_to_variable = { CHI_economy_research_speed_factor = -0.04 tooltip = research_speed_factor_tt }
			add_to_variable = { CHI_economy_civilian_factories_productivity = -0.04 tooltip = civilian_factories_productivity_tt }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CHI_semiconductor_backwardness_3 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = { localization_key = modifies_dynamic_modifier_tt MODIFIER = CHI_economy_modifier }
			add_to_variable = { CHI_economy_research_speed_factor = -0.02 tooltip = research_speed_factor_tt }
			add_to_variable = { CHI_economy_civilian_factories_productivity = -0.02 tooltip = civilian_factories_productivity_tt }
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = { localization_key = modifies_dynamic_modifier_tt MODIFIER = CHI_economy_modifier }
			add_to_variable = { CHI_economy_microchip_export_multiplier_modifier = 0.10 tooltip = microchip_export_multiplier_modifier_tt }
			add_to_variable = { CHI_economy_trade_opinion_factor = 0.05 tooltip = trade_opinion_factor_tt }
			add_to_variable = { CHI_economy_resource_export_multiplier_modifier = 0.04 tooltip = resource_export_multiplier_modifier_tt }
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = USA }
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = chi_semiconductor_supremacy }
			}
		}
	}

}

country_event = {
	id = CHI_space_events.13
	title = CHI_space_events.13.t
	desc = CHI_space_events.13.d
	picture = x
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = CHI_space_events.13.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CHI_space_events.13.a executed"
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CHI_lunar_satellite_invest }
			custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_lunar_satellite_invest_tt
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = CHI_space_events_lunar_satellite
				bonus = 0.50
				uses = 2
				category = CAT_satellite
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CHI_lunar_rocketry_invest }
			custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_lunar_rocketry_invest_tt
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = CHI_space_events_lunar_rocketry
				bonus = 0.50
				uses = 2
				category = CAT_missile
			}
		}
		newline = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = { localization_key = modifies_dynamic_modifier_tt MODIFIER = CHI_economy_modifier }
		add_to_variable = { CHI_economy_research_speed_factor = 0.03 tooltip = research_speed_factor_tt }
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
	}

}

country_event = {
	id = CHI_political_events.8
	title = CHI_political_events.8.t
	desc = CHI_political_events.8.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = CHI_political_events.8.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CHI_political_events.8.a"
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				add_tech_bonus = {
					name = strategy_of_invigorating_through_STE
					bonus = 0.3
					uses = 1
					category = CAT_internet_tech
				}
			}
			50 = {
				add_tech_bonus = {
					name = strategy_of_invigorating_through_STE
					bonus = 0.3
					uses = 1
					category = CAT_computing_tech
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						NOT = { has_completed_focus = CHI_hu_jintao_reign }
						NOT = { has_completed_focus = CHI_zeng_qinghong_reign }
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = CHI_political_events.8
					days = 365
				}
			}
		}
	}

}

	desc = CHI_political_events.51.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = CHI_political_events.51.a

			limit = { check_variable = { CHI_demographic_policy_stage = 1 } }
			activate_mission = CHI_grey_society_crisis

		}
		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
	}

}
